 Political background Balasore is a Lok Sabha seat in Odisha where BJP has won the election thrice
 is seat par biju janata dal ne 2014 main pehali baar jeet hasil kii
 In the initial Lok Sabha elections after independence, the Congress ruled here
 1951, 57 or 62 kaa chunaav congress ne jeeta
 In 1967 the CPI opened its account on this seat and Samarendra Kundu emerged victorious
 1971 main congress ne yahaan phir vaapasi kii
 After the anti-indira wave in 1977, the Congress lost from here and Samarendra Kundu won the elections once again
 1980 or 84 main congress kaa paracham is seat par phir fahraaya
 Samarendra Kundu won elections on the Janata Dal ticket in the 1989 election
 1991 or 96 main yah seat congress ke khate main gai
 In the era of atal-advani, this seat was lotus fed
 1998, 99 or 2004 main yahaan bijepi ke tikat par kharbela swen chunaav jite
 In 2009, the Congress benefited from the break-up in the alliance between the BJD and the BJP and Srikanth Jena won from this seat on the Congress ticket
 haalanki 2014 main yahaan se bijedy ke rabindra kumaar jena vijayi hue
 Recently Srikanth Jena has been removed from the primary membership of the party by Congress President Rahul Gandhi for anti-party activities
 haalanki jena pichley saal disambar main hi pradesh congress cameti se istipha de chuke the
 After his removal from the party, Srikanth Jena accused Odisha Pradesh Congress Committee President Niranjan Patnaik of being involved in the mining scam
 shrikant jena ne congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi par bhi hamalaa kiya tha or kaha tha ki agar vah rahul gandhi kii pole kholenge to vah munh dikhaane laayak nahin rah jaaenge

 dharmasindhu naamak granth main kaha gaya he ki 'paredeurnishithaikadesh-vyaptu purvedyuh sampoorntadvyaptu purvaiv
 
 'tippaniyan The meaning of these lines in Hindi is that if Chaturdashi stays for some time in the Nishith period on the next day and the whole day on the first day, then Mahashivratri should be observed on the very first day
 Maha Shivratri 2018: tasveeron main dekhie desh main kaise manaai ja rahi he mahashivaratri This year, on 13 February, the whole day was Trayodashi and Chaturdashi has started from 11
35 am to midnight
 aaj 14 farvari ko puure din or raat 12:47 minute tak chaturdashi rahegi In such a situation, Shivaratri can be worshiped on 14 February
 aaj 14 farvari ko mahashivaratri kaa paaran hoga
 Passing time will be from 07:04 in the morning to 15:20 in the afternoon
 aasthaa se judi anya khabaron ke liye yahaan clic karen
 If you have not worshiped Lord Shiva at Shivaratri on February 13, then you can please Lord Bholenath on February 14
 jab do dinon main shivaratri ho to kis din shivaratri manaai jaae iskaa granthon main ullekh kiya gaya he
 In the book called Dharmasindhu it is said that 'paredyurnishithachadesh-vyaptau puraveduya: sampoornatdhupayatau purave

 haryana ke hisar jile kii barwaala vidhansabha seat kaa itihaas kaaphi rochak he
 The mlas, once formed from this seat, have never been able to reach the assembly again
 itnaa hi nahin raajnneetik dal bhi kisi vijeta ummidavaar ko dobaaraa maidan main utaarne se parhez karte hai

 isi kaa nateeja he ki barwaala se ek baar jeeta hua vidhayak dobaaraa se vidhansabha kaa munh nahin dekh paaya

 bijepi ke ummidavaar surendra punia ne apni jeet kaa daawa kar rahe hai
